| <a id="peace-ai-evaluate-other-if-core"></a> PEACE\_AI\_EVALUATE\_OTHER\_IF\_CORE | true | Whether AI should evaluate giving states to other winners if state is their core (may affect performance on new conference turn) |  |
| <a id="peace-ai-evaluate-other-if-claim"></a> PEACE\_AI\_EVALUATE\_OTHER\_IF\_CLAIM | true | Whether AI should evaluate giving states to other winners if they have a claim on the state (may affect performance on new conference turn) |  |
| <a id="peace-ai-evaluate-other-always"></a> PEACE\_AI\_EVALUATE\_OTHER\_ALWAYS | false | Whether AI should always evaluate giving states to other winners (!!! may heavily affect performance on new conference turn for large peace conferences !!!) |  |
| <a id="division-supply-ratio-to-motorize"></a> DIVISION\_SUPPLY\_RATIO\_TO\_MOTORIZE | 0.80 | If supply ratio is less than this, consider motorizing any applicable nearby supply hub |  |
| <a id="industrial-org-trait-unlock-randomness"></a> INDUSTRIAL\_ORG\_TRAIT\_UNLOCK\_RANDOMNESS | 3 | AI will pick a random from N top traits when choosing a trait to unlock |  |
| <a id="industrial-org-policy-change-randomness"></a> INDUSTRIAL\_ORG\_POLICY\_CHANGE\_RANDOMNESS | 3 | AI will pick a random from N top policies when choosing a policy to attach to an MIO |  |
| <a id="industrial-org-research-assign-randomness"></a> INDUSTRIAL\_ORG\_RESEARCH\_ASSIGN\_RANDOMNESS | 3 | AI will pick a random from N top MIOs when choosing an MIO to assign to a research |  |
| <a id="industrial-org-production-assign-randomness"></a> INDUSTRIAL\_ORG\_PRODUCTION\_ASSIGN\_RANDOMNESS | 3 | AI will pick a random from N top MIOs when choosing an MIO to assign to a production line |  |
| <a id="industrial-org-policy-change-scale"></a> INDUSTRIAL\_ORG\_POLICY\_CHANGE\_SCALE | 1.0 | Policy change weight will be scaled by this value |  |
| <a id="industrial-org-trait-rank-factor"></a> INDUSTRIAL\_ORG\_TRAIT\_RANK\_FACTOR | 0.80 | When precomputing weights, traits will affect the final score less the further down the tree they are, by this factor |  |
| <a id="industrial-org-research-bonus-factor"></a> INDUSTRIAL\_ORG\_RESEARCH\_BONUS\_FACTOR | 1.0 | Research bonus will be multiplied by this factor when evaluating design teams |  |
| <a id="ai-wanted-land-based-planes-factor"></a> AI\_WANTED\_LAND\_BASED\_PLANES\_FACTOR | 0.50 | Factor applied to desire for land based planes (total airbase space \* define) |  |
| <a id="ai-wanted-carrier-based-planes-factor"></a> AI\_WANTED\_CARRIER\_BASED\_PLANES\_FACTOR | 1.0 | Factor applied to desire for carrier based planes (total carrier space \* define) |  |

## <a id="nfocus"></a>NFocus
| Name | Default | Developer comment | Usage |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| <a id="focus-point-days"></a> FOCUS\_POINT\_DAYS | 7 | Each point takes a week |  |
| <a id="focus-progress-peace"></a> FOCUS\_PROGRESS\_PEACE | 1 | Progress during peace |  |
| <a id="focus-progress-war"></a> FOCUS\_PROGRESS\_WAR | 1 | Progress during war |  |
| <a id="max-saved-focus-progress"></a> MAX\_SAVED\_FOCUS\_PROGRESS | 10 | This much progress can be saved while not having a focus selected |  |

## <a id="noperatives"></a>NOperatives
| Name | Default | Developer comment | Usage |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| <a id="agency-creation-days"></a> AGENCY\_CREATION\_DAYS | 30 | Number of days needed to create an intelligence agency |  |
| <a id="agency-upgrade-days"></a> AGENCY\_UPGRADE\_DAYS | 30 | Number of days needed to upgrade an intelligence agency |  |
| <a id="agency-creation-factories"></a> AGENCY\_CREATION\_FACTORIES | 5 | Number of factories used to create an intelligence agency |  |
| <a id="agency-ai-base-num-factories"></a> AGENCY\_AI\_BASE\_NUM\_FACTORIES | 25.0 | Used by AI to pace the upgrades. Formula : if( AGENCY\_AI\_BASE\_NUM\_FACTORIES <= num\_civ\_factories - num\_upgrades \* AGENCY\_AI\_PER\_UPGRADE\_FACTORIES ) |  |
| <a id="agency-ai-per-upgrade-factories"></a> AGENCY\_AI\_PER\_UPGRADE\_FACTORIES | 6.0 | Used by AI to pace the upgrades. Formula : if( AGENCY\_AI\_BASE\_NUM\_FACTORIES <= num\_civ\_factories - num\_upgrades \* AGENCY\_AI\_PER\_UPGRADE\_FACTORIES ) |  |
| <a id="agency-upgrade-per-operative-slot"></a> AGENCY\_UPGRADE\_PER\_OPERATIVE\_SLOT | 5 | Number of upgrade needed to unlock an additional operative slot |  |
| <a id="max-operative-slot-from-agency-upgrades"></a> MAX\_OPERATIVE\_SLOT\_FROM\_AGENCY\_UPGRADES | 1 | max operative slots gained from upgrades |  |
| <a id="agency-operative-recruitment-time"></a> AGENCY\_OPERATIVE\_RECRUITMENT\_TIME | 30 | Number of days to wait to have operative to recruit when an operative slot first becomes available |  |
| <a id="become-spymaster-pp-cost"></a> BECOME\_SPYMASTER\_PP\_COST | 50 | Number of political power used to become Spy Master |  |
| <a id="become-spymaster-min-upgrades"></a> BECOME\_SPYMASTER\_MIN\_UPGRADES | 3 | Number of agency upgrades you need before becoming Spy Master |  |
| <a id="base-counter-intelligence-rating"></a> BASE\_COUNTER\_INTELLIGENCE\_RATING | 0.0 | Base national counter intelligence rating for all countries |  |
| <a id="agency-defense-effect-on-hostile-action-cost"></a> AGENCY\_DEFENSE\_EFFECT\_ON\_HOSTILE\_ACTION\_COST | 0.2 | Defense factor that is responsible for multiplying the cost hostile actions against our country by its level and this value |  |
| <a id="intel-network-gain-rate-on-wrong-controller"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_GAIN\_RATE\_ON\_WRONG\_CONTROLLER | -10.0 | Amount of network strength lost in a state when it does not have the right controller anymore |  |
| <a id="intel-network-gain-rate-on-out-of-range"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_GAIN\_RATE\_ON\_OUT\_OF\_RANGE | -1.75 | Amount of network strength lost in a state that has the right controller but is out of range of any operative |  |
| <a id="intel-network-gain-from-adjacency-factor"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_GAIN\_FROM\_ADJACENCY\_FACTOR | 0.5 | Factor multiplied to the sum of the positive difference between a state's strength and its neighbors'. In other words, how strongly neighbors impact the strength gained in a state. Values greater or equal to 1 are discouraged. |  |
| <a id="intel-network-gain-decay-per-step-factor"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_GAIN\_DECAY\_PER\_STEP\_FACTOR | 0.5 | Factor multiplied to the gain of the previous node in the netowrk initially contributed by the agent. In other words, before adjacency, the strength gain in a state would be GainFromOperative \* ( INTEL\_NETWORK\_GAIN\_DECAY\_PER\_STEP\_FACTOR ^ NodeDepth ) where NodeDepth is the distance between the state and the operative's location. |  |
| <a id="intel-network-strength-target-offset-per-operative"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_STRENGTH\_TARGET\_OFFSET\_PER\_OPERATIVE | 15.0 | The amount of strength each operative on build intel network mission in a sub network add to the base target network strength |  |
| <a id="intel-network-strength-decay-when-above-target"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_STRENGTH\_DECAY\_WHEN\_ABOVE\_TARGET | -2.5 | The amount of strength removed each tick from a state that has more strength than the target |  |
| <a id="intel-network-base-strength-target-counterintelligence-factor"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_BASE\_STRENGTH\_TARGET\_COUNTERINTELLIGENCE\_FACTOR | -10.0 | BaseStrengthTarget = Factor \* CounterIntelligenceRating + Offset |  |
| <a id="intel-network-base-strength-target-counterintelligence-offset"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_BASE\_STRENGTH\_TARGET\_COUNTERINTELLIGENCE\_OFFSET | 90 | Offset mentioned above |  |
| <a id="intel-network-min-vp-to-target"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_MIN\_VP\_TO\_TARGET | 15 | The minimum value of the highest VP in a state to consider the state as a valid target to start building an intel network |  |
| <a id="intel-network-min-strength-to-target"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_MIN\_STRENGTH\_TO\_TARGET | 101.0 | The minimum value of the intel network in a state to consider it a valid target to deploy an operative in |  |
| <a id="intel-network-min-strength-to-link-subnetworks"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_MIN\_STRENGTH\_TO\_LINK\_SUBNETWORKS | 0.0 | Where the influence of two operative meet, the two nodes on each side have to have strictly more than the given strength before the two operatives have a chance of being considered in the same network |  |
| <a id="intel-network-operative-gain-stacking-factor"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_OPERATIVE\_GAIN\_STACKING\_FACTOR | 0.5 | When multiple operative are present in the same location, this factor is applied for each operative with a lower gain than the max. So if operatives have the gain [ 3, 1, 2 ] in the same location, it is sorted to [ 1, 2, 3 ] then converted to [ 1\*D^2, 2\*D^1, 3 ], with D being this define, so if D=0.5 we have [ 0.25, 1, 3 ] and the final gain from operative at this location will be 4.25. Putting this define to 0 is equivalent to considering the maximum value only. |  |
| <a id="intel-network-min-strength-for-state-to-count-toward-national-coverage"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_MIN\_STRENGTH\_FOR\_STATE\_TO\_COUNT\_TOWARD\_NATIONAL\_COVERAGE | 0.0 | Amount of strength (0, 100) in a state required for it to count toward the national coverage |  |
| <a id="intel-network-national-coverage-controlled-states-weight"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_NATIONAL\_COVERAGE\_CONTROLLED\_STATES\_WEIGHT | 0.2 | Weight (expected [0,1]) multiplied by the number of states covered by the network that are controlled by the target over the total number of states the target controls |  |
| <a id="intel-network-national-coverage-core-states-weight"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_NATIONAL\_COVERAGE\_CORE\_STATES\_WEIGHT | 0.6 | Weight (expected [0,1]) multiplied by the number of states covered by the network that are core to the target over the total number of states the target has for core |  |
| <a id="intel-network-national-coverage-owned-worth-weight"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_NATIONAL\_COVERAGE\_OWNED\_WORTH\_WEIGHT | 0.2 | Weight (expected [0,1]) multiplied by the value of victory points covered by the network over the total value of victory points controlled by the targets |  |
| <a id="intel-network-occupied-tag-states-weight"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_OCCUPIED\_TAG\_STATES\_WEIGHT | 0.5 | Weight (expected [0,1]) multiplied to the fraction of number of state covered by the intel network divided by the number of states occupied by the target of the network, per occupied tag |  |
| <a id="intel-network-occupied-tag-worth-weight"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_OCCUPIED\_TAG\_WORTH\_WEIGHT | 0.5 | Weight (expected [0,1]) multiplied to the fraction of victory points worth of states covered by the intel network divided by the worth of states occupied by the target of the network, per occupied tag |  |
| <a id="intel-network-min-sub-network-size-for-detection"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_MIN\_SUB\_NETWORK\_SIZE\_FOR\_DETECTION | 0 | minimum number of state of a sub-intel network before an operative on build intel network mission in this network can be detected |  |
| <a id="intel-network-min-national-coverage-for-detection"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_MIN\_NATIONAL\_COVERAGE\_FOR\_DETECTION | 0.02 | [0, 1] minimum national coverage required for an operative on build intel network to have a chance to be discovered |  |
| <a id="intel-network-min-sub-network-national-coverage-for-detection"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_MIN\_SUB\_NETWORK\_NATIONAL\_COVERAGE\_FOR\_DETECTION | 0.01 | [0, 1] minimum national coverage of the network the operative on build intel network is in to have a chance to be discovered |  |
| <a id="intel-network-min-sub-network-strength-for-detection"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_MIN\_SUB\_NETWORK\_STRENGTH\_FOR\_DETECTION | 10.0 | [0, 100] minimum network strength of the network the operative on build intel network mission is in to have a chance to be discovered |  |
| <a id="intel-network-intelligence-agency-defense-to-detection-factor"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_INTELLIGENCE\_AGENCY\_DEFENSE\_TO\_DETECTION\_FACTOR | 2.0 | multiplied to the intelligence agency defense of the target of the intel network |  |
| <a id="intel-network-intelligence-agency-defense-detection-scale-factor"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_INTELLIGENCE\_AGENCY\_DEFENSE\_DETECTION\_SCALE\_FACTOR | 0.0 | factor multiplied to the intelligence agency defense of the target of the intel network before being factored to the detection chance |  |
| <a id="intel-network-max-intelligence-agency-defense-detection-scale-factor"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_MAX\_INTELLIGENCE\_AGENCY\_DEFENSE\_DETECTION\_SCALE\_FACTOR | 1.0 | clamp the value from the multiplication of the above factor (expect a value greater or equal to 1) |  |
| <a id="intel-network-national-coverage-to-detection-chance-factor"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_NATIONAL\_COVERAGE\_TO\_DETECTION\_CHANCE\_FACTOR | 1.0 | multiplied to the national coverage (a value in range [0, 1] |  |
| <a id="intel-network-sub-network-strength-to-detection-chance-factor"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_SUB\_NETWORK\_STRENGTH\_TO\_DETECTION\_CHANCE\_FACTOR | 0.1 | multiplied to the network strength (a value in range [0, 100] |  |
| <a id="intel-network-sub-network-national-coverage-to-detection-chance-factor"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_SUB\_NETWORK\_NATIONAL\_COVERAGE\_TO\_DETECTION\_CHANCE\_FACTOR | 3.0 | multiplied to the contribution to the national coverage of the sub network (a value in range [0, 1]) |  |
| <a id="intel-network-detection-global-factor"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_DETECTION\_GLOBAL\_FACTOR | 0.01 | global factor multiplied to the detection chance before it is multiplied a dice roll in the range [0,1000) |  |
| <a id="build-intel-network-daily-xp-gain"></a> BUILD\_INTEL\_NETWORK\_DAILY\_XP\_GAIN | 1 |  |  |
| <a id="quiet-intel-network-daily-xp-gain"></a> QUIET\_INTEL\_NETWORK\_DAILY\_XP\_GAIN | 0 |  |  |
| <a id="operative-mission-detection-chance-factor"></a> OPERATIVE\_MISSION\_DETECTION\_CHANCE\_FACTOR | { 0.0, 1.0, 1.0, 1.0, 0.0, 3.0, 0.1, 0.1, 3.0 } | Factor multiplied to the detection chance of an agent on mission before the offsets NoMission BuildIntelNetwork QuietIntelNetwork CounterIntelligence RootOutResistance BoostIdeology ControlTrade DiplomaticPressure Propaganda |  |
| <a id="operative-slots-from-faction-members-for-spy-master"></a> OPERATIVE\_SLOTS\_FROM\_FACTION\_MEMBERS\_FOR\_SPY\_MASTER | { 0.0, 0.0, 0.25, 10.0, 0.5, 50.0 } | used for calculating how many operatives will a spy master gain from its faction members first number in every now is number of operatives gained second number is total factory needed (mil and civ) for giving previous ratio 0 operative for [0, 10) 0.25 operative for [10, 50) 0.5 operative for >= 50 |  |
| <a id="intel-network-state-modifier-strength-threshold"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_STATE\_MODIFIER\_STRENGTH\_THRESHOLD | 10 | Minimum amount of strength required in a state for the intel network related modifiers to start being applied |  |
| <a id="intel-network-min-default-for-showing"></a> INTEL\_NETWORK\_MIN\_DEFAULT\_FOR\_SHOWING | 25 | default min level for networks used to filter operation requirements if not overriden |  |
| <a id="operative-base-intel-network-gain"></a> OPERATIVE\_BASE\_INTEL\_NETWORK\_GAIN | 0.4 | Base amount of network strength gain per day provided by an operative |  |
| <a id="operative-max-intel-network-gain"></a> OPERATIVE\_MAX\_INTEL\_NETWORK\_GAIN | -1.0 | Max amount of network strength gain per day provided by an operative after modifiers have been applied (negative value means no max) |  |
| <a id="counter-intelligence-foreign-agent-factor"></a> COUNTER\_INTELLIGENCE\_FOREIGN\_AGENT\_FACTOR | 0.0 | Multiplier to the counter intelligence provided by foreign (ally) operatives |  |
| <a id="counter-intelligence-stacking-factor"></a> COUNTER\_INTELLIGENCE\_STACKING\_FACTOR | 0.5 | Multiplier applied to each operative after the first one. So if we have the following counter intelligence rating values [ 0.1, 0.3, 0.2 ], the factor is applied twice for the lowest value and once for the 2nd lowest one as such : [ 0.3, 0.2 \* D, 0.1 \* D \* D ] and then the result is summed up to give the final rating value |  |
| <a id="counter-intelligence-to-defense-log-factor"></a> COUNTER\_INTELLIGENCE\_TO\_DEFENSE\_LOG\_FACTOR | 0.0 | Defense = LogFactor \* log( 1 + CounterIntelligence ) + CounterIntelligence / Divisor |  |
| <a id="counter-intelligence-to-defense-divisor"></a> COUNTER\_INTELLIGENCE\_TO\_DEFENSE\_DIVISOR | 1.0 | see above |  |
| <a id="counter-intelligence-daily-xp-gain"></a> COUNTER\_INTELLIGENCE\_DAILY\_XP\_GAIN | 0.112 |  |  |
| <a id="boost-ideology-national-coverage-factor"></a> BOOST\_IDEOLOGY\_NATIONAL\_COVERAGE\_FACTOR | 1.0 | used to compute the drift factor as follow: BASE \* SUB\_NETWORK\_NC \* BOOST\_IDEOLOGY\_DEFENSE\_FACTOR |  |
| <a id="boost-ideology-max-drift-by-operative"></a> BOOST\_IDEOLOGY\_MAX\_DRIFT\_BY\_OPERATIVE | 0.25 | the maximum drift an operative can cause, a negative value means no maximum |  |
| <a id="boost-ideology-drift-stacking-factor"></a> BOOST\_IDEOLOGY\_DRIFT\_STACKING\_FACTOR | 0.5 | multiplied to the drift of an operative for each operative after the first one, with the greatest drift. So if we have the following drift values [ 0.1, 0.3, 0.2 ], the factor is applied twice for the lowest value and once for the 2nd lowest one as such : [ 0.3, 0.2 \* D, 0.1 \* D \* D ] and then the result is summed up to give the final drift value. |  |
| <a id="boost-ideology-defense-factor"></a> BOOST\_IDEOLOGY\_DEFENSE\_FACTOR | 0.2 | multiplied to the target's defense to get the amount of drift to remove from each operative's drift |  |
| <a id="boost-ideology-daily-xp-gain"></a> BOOST\_IDEOLOGY\_DAILY\_XP\_GAIN | 0.274 |  |  |

| <a id="propaganda-country-stacking-factor"></a> PROPAGANDA\_COUNTRY\_STACKING\_FACTOR | 0.5 | Multiplied to the Stability/WarSupport drift values of each country after the one with the greatest values. The process is done separatly for Stability and WarSupport |  |
| <a id="propaganda-daily-xp-gain"></a> PROPAGANDA\_DAILY\_XP\_GAIN | 0.350 |  |  |

| <a id="control-trade-stacking-factor"></a> CONTROL\_TRADE\_STACKING\_FACTOR | 0.5 | Multiplied to the drift of each operative after the first one |  |

| <a id="operative-base-diplomatic-pressure-ai-acceptance-score-drift"></a> OPERATIVE\_BASE\_DIPLOMATIC\_PRESSURE\_AI\_ACCEPTANCE\_SCORE\_DRIFT | 0.4 | The daily change in the amount of opinion requiered to join a faction |  |

| <a id="diplomatic-pressure-max-ai-acceptance-score-increase"></a> DIPLOMATIC\_PRESSURE\_MAX\_AI\_ACCEPTANCE\_SCORE\_INCREASE | 20.0 | the maximum amount of ai acceptance score from diplomatic pressure |  |
| <a id="diplomatic-pressure-max-tension-requirements-decrease"></a> DIPLOMATIC\_PRESSURE\_MAX\_TENSION\_REQUIREMENTS\_DECREASE | 0.20 | amount of tension (tensions is in range [0,1]) that can be removed from the requirements imposed by the modifier join\_faction\_tension\_limit |  |
| <a id="diplomatic-pressure-operative-stacking-factor"></a> DIPLOMATIC\_PRESSURE\_OPERATIVE\_STACKING\_FACTOR | 0.5 | The diminishing return factor to apply to operative working for the same faction after the first one. Operatives operating for a same faction are ranked by their efficiency and their opinion and tension drift are individually applyied a stacking factor like so: DRIFT \* STACKING\_FACTOR^RANK where RANK is a value from 0 to the number of operative -1 where the opperative with the highest drift value has rank 0 |  |
| <a id="diplomatic-pressure-ai-acceptance-score-decay"></a> DIPLOMATIC\_PRESSURE\_AI\_ACCEPTANCE\_SCORE\_DECAY | 0.4 | daily decay when the mission is not active |  |

| <a id="min-national-coverage-for-propaganda"></a> MIN\_NATIONAL\_COVERAGE\_FOR\_PROPAGANDA | 0.01 | Minimum network coverage required to start the mission (the code ensures that a network exists at all) |  |

## <a id="nintel"></a>NIntel
| Name | Default | Developer comment | Usage |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| <a id="country-level-intel-maximums"></a> COUNTRY\_LEVEL\_INTEL\_MAXIMUMS | { 100.0, 100.0, 100.0, 100.0 } | The maximum intel a country can have over another Civilian Army Navy Airforce |  |
| <a id="static-intel-source-operation-tokens-maximums"></a> STATIC\_INTEL\_SOURCE\_OPERATION\_TOKENS\_MAXIMUMS | { } | Static sources: A static source is a source that will fully decay once its origin disappear. (e.g. radar destroyed) MAXIMUMS: if set to an non-empty arrays, overrides COUNTRY\_LEVEL\_INTEL\_MAXIMUMS for this specific source (note that COUNTRY\_LEVEL\_INTEL\_MAXIMUMS is applied after INTEL\_SOURCE\_XXX\_MAXIMUMS) |  |
| <a id="static-intel-source-broken-cypher-maximums"></a> STATIC\_INTEL\_SOURCE\_BROKEN\_CYPHER\_MAXIMUMS | { 60.0, 60.0, 60.0, 60.0 } |  |  |
| <a id="static-intel-source-radar-maximums"></a> STATIC\_INTEL\_SOURCE\_RADAR\_MAXIMUMS | { 10.0, 10.0, 20.0, 20.0 } |  |  |
| <a id="static-intel-source-intel-network-maximums"></a> STATIC\_INTEL\_SOURCE\_INTEL\_NETWORK\_MAXIMUMS | { 30.0, 30.0, 40.0, 30.0 } |  |  |
| <a id="dynamic-intel-source-event-flat-decay"></a> DYNAMIC\_INTEL\_SOURCE\_EVENT\_FLAT\_DECAY | 0.0 | Dynamic intel pool can be manipulated through the following defines: FLAT\_DECAY and MULT\_DECAY control the rate at which the intel decays The formula is applied as follow (runs daily): NextIntel = ( Intel - FLAT\_DECAY ) \* MULT\_DECAY AGGREGAT\_LOG\_FACTOR and AGGREGAT\_DIVISOR control the rate at which intel accumulates. It is applied to the sum of the intel generated throughout the day as follow: Aggregat = LOG\_FACTOR \* log( 1 + IntelOfTheDay ) + IntelOfTheDay / DIVISOR The Aggregat is then added to the pool of intel. If DIVISOR is zero then the division is evaluated to zero. MAXIMUMS controls the maximum value that the pool can contribute to the final intel values. ABSOLUTE\_MAXIMUMS defines a ceiling for the intel in the pool that will never be exceeded. They are meant to be greater or equal to MAXIMUMS. If the array is empty, no absolute maximum is defined. Dynamic pool EVENT |  |

## <a id="nsupply"></a>NSupply
| Name | Default | Developer comment | Usage |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| <a id="max-railway-level"></a> MAX\_RAILWAY\_LEVEL | 5 | update railway texture as well, each frame corresponds to a level |  |
| <a id="capital-supply-base"></a> CAPITAL\_SUPPLY\_BASE | 5.0 | defines to calculate the capitals supply. This will be also used for max supply of other nodes depending on how well they are connected to capital. Using the formula: CapitalSupply = CAPITAL\_SUPPLY\_BASE + (NumberOfCivilianFactories \* CAPITAL\_SUPPLY\_CIVILIAN\_FACTORIES) + (NumberOfMilitaryFactories \* CAPITAL\_SUPPLY\_MILITARY\_FACTORIES) + (NumberOfDockyards \* CAPITAL\_SUPPLY\_DOCKYARDS) base supply for capital |  |
| <a id="capital-supply-civilian-factories"></a> CAPITAL\_SUPPLY\_CIVILIAN\_FACTORIES | 0.3 | supply from one civilian factory |  |
| <a id="capital-supply-military-factories"></a> CAPITAL\_SUPPLY\_MILITARY\_FACTORIES | 0.6 | supply from one military factory |  |
| <a id="capital-supply-dockyards"></a> CAPITAL\_SUPPLY\_DOCKYARDS | 0.4 | supply from one naval factory |  |
| <a id="capital-initial-supply-flow"></a> CAPITAL\_INITIAL\_SUPPLY\_FLOW | 5.0 | defines that are used for supply reach for capital supply flow will start from INITIAL\_SUPPLY\_FLOW and will be reduced by a penalty on each province it travels (which depends on how far we are from our origin, terrain etc) a supply reach >= 1.0 considered "perfect" and will be able to fully support units on that particular province (assuming you are not over capacity) starting supply from |  |
| <a id="capital-starting-penalty-per-province"></a> CAPITAL\_STARTING\_PENALTY\_PER\_PROVINCE | 0.5 | starting penalty that will be added as supply moves away from its origin (modified by stuff like terrain) |  |
| <a id="capital-added-penalty-per-province"></a> CAPITAL\_ADDED\_PENALTY\_PER\_PROVINCE | 1.2 | added penalty as we move away from origin |  |
| <a id="node-initial-supply-flow"></a> NODE\_INITIAL\_SUPPLY\_FLOW | 2.8 | defines that are used for supply reach for built nodes |  |
| <a id="node-starting-penalty-per-province"></a> NODE\_STARTING\_PENALTY\_PER\_PROVINCE | 0.50 |  |  |
| <a id="node-added-penalty-per-province"></a> NODE\_ADDED\_PENALTY\_PER\_PROVINCE | 0.70 |  |  |
| <a id="naval-base-initial-supply-flow"></a> NAVAL\_BASE\_INITIAL\_SUPPLY\_FLOW | 3.3 | defines that are used for supply reach for dockyards |  |
| <a id="naval-base-starting-penalty-per-province"></a> NAVAL\_BASE\_STARTING\_PENALTY\_PER\_PROVINCE | 0.84 |  |  |
| <a id="naval-base-added-penalty-per-province"></a> NAVAL\_BASE\_ADDED\_PENALTY\_PER\_PROVINCE | 1.1 |  |  |
| <a id="node-flow-bonus-per-rail-level"></a> NODE\_FLOW\_BONUS\_PER\_RAIL\_LEVEL | 0.34 | Node Flow (i.e. province caps) increase by this amount per railway level of the node's bottleneck |  |
| <a id="river-railway-level"></a> RIVER\_RAILWAY\_LEVEL | 1 | rivers will transfer in between nodes as if they were this level |  |
| <a id="floating-harbor-initial-supply-flow"></a> FLOATING\_HARBOR\_INITIAL\_SUPPLY\_FLOW | 2.6 | defines that are used for supply reach for floating harbors |  |
| <a id="floating-harbor-starting-penalty-per-province"></a> FLOATING\_HARBOR\_STARTING\_PENALTY\_PER\_PROVINCE | 0.8 |  |  |
| <a id="floating-harbor-added-penalty-per-province"></a> FLOATING\_HARBOR\_ADDED\_PENALTY\_PER\_PROVINCE | 0.8 |  |  |
| <a id="floating-harbor-base-supply"></a> FLOATING\_HARBOR\_BASE\_SUPPLY | 15.0 | supply given by a floating harbor |  |
| <a id="floating-harbor-base-duration"></a> FLOATING\_HARBOR\_BASE\_DURATION | 21 | duration of a full hp floating harbor |  |
| <a id="floating-harbor-duration-ratio-at-min-hp"></a> FLOATING\_HARBOR\_DURATION\_RATIO\_AT\_MIN\_HP | 0.0 | duration mult for a harbor that was reduced to 0 hp |  |
| <a id="floating-harbor-min-decay"></a> FLOATING\_HARBOR\_MIN\_DECAY | 0.2 | Always reduce Floating Harbor longevity by this many "hours" per hour |  |
| <a id="floating-harbor-decay-max-air-bonus"></a> FLOATING\_HARBOR\_DECAY\_MAX\_AIR\_BONUS | -0.1 | At 100% Friendly Air superiourity, change decay rate by this many "hours" per hour |  |
| <a id="floating-harbor-decay-max-air-penalty"></a> FLOATING\_HARBOR\_DECAY\_MAX\_AIR\_PENALTY | 0.4 | At 100% Enemy Air superiourity, change decay rate by this many "hours" per hour |  |
| <a id="floating-harbor-decay-max-naval-bonus"></a> FLOATING\_HARBOR\_DECAY\_MAX\_NAVAL\_BONUS | -0.2 | At 100% Friendly naval superiourity, change decay rate by this many "hours" per hour |  |
| <a id="floating-harbor-decay-max-naval-penalty"></a> FLOATING\_HARBOR\_DECAY\_MAX\_NAVAL\_PENALTY | 0.5 | At 100% Enemy Naval superiourity, change decay rate by this many "hours" per hour |  |
| <a id="floating-harbor-decay-no-control-penalty"></a> FLOATING\_HARBOR\_DECAY\_NO\_CONTROL\_PENALTY | 1.0 | If adjacent land province is not held, change decay rate by this many "hours" per hour |  |
| <a id="supply-flow-drop-reduction-at-max-infra"></a> SUPPLY\_FLOW\_DROP\_REDUCTION\_AT\_MAX\_INFRA | 0.30 | max infrastructure level will reduce the supply flow drop off by this ratio |  |
| <a id="supply-flow-penalty-crossing-rivers"></a> SUPPLY\_FLOW\_PENALTY\_CROSSING\_RIVERS | 0.20 | crossing rivers introduces additional penalty |  |
| <a id="supply-flow-dist-logistics-falloff-k"></a> SUPPLY\_FLOW\_DIST\_LOGISTICS\_FALLOFF\_K | 1.3 | node flow terrain falloff is scaled by logistics curve based on distance(d) (scalar / (1+e^(-k(d-midpoint)))) How steep the curve is |  |
| <a id="supply-flow-dist-logistics-falloff-midpoint"></a> SUPPLY\_FLOW\_DIST\_LOGISTICS\_FALLOFF\_MIDPOINT | 2.3 | sigmoid inflection point |  |
| <a id="supply-flow-dist-logistics-falloff-scalar"></a> SUPPLY\_FLOW\_DIST\_LOGISTICS\_FALLOFF\_SCALAR | 0.9 | Max Penalty adjustment due to distance |  |
| <a id="supply-flow-dist-logistics-falloff-min-penalty-scale"></a> SUPPLY\_FLOW\_DIST\_LOGISTICS\_FALLOFF\_MIN\_PENALTY\_SCALE | 0.25 | Logistics curve never reduces penalty facor below this limit |  |
| <a id="supply-hub-full-motorization-bonus"></a> SUPPLY\_HUB\_FULL\_MOTORIZATION\_BONUS | 2.2 | The range bonus added to a fully motorized hub. This supply is added on top of the XXX\_INITIAL\_SUPPLY\_FLOW defined above. |  |
| <a id="supply-hub-full-motorization-truck-cost"></a> SUPPLY\_HUB\_FULL\_MOTORIZATION\_TRUCK\_COST | 60.0 | How many trucks does it cost to fully motorize a hub |  |
| <a id="supply-hub-motorization-marginal-effect-decay"></a> SUPPLY\_HUB\_MOTORIZATION\_MARGINAL\_EFFECT\_DECAY | 1.6 | For each additional level of motorization on a hub (i.e. contry with set motoriazation) reduce max bonus for next level by this amount |  |
| <a id="railway-base-flow"></a> RAILWAY\_BASE\_FLOW | 10.0 | used for calculating "flow" for railways. how much base flow railway gives when a node connected to its capital/a naval node by a railway |  |
| <a id="railway-flow-per-level"></a> RAILWAY\_FLOW\_PER\_LEVEL | 5.0 | how much additional flow a railway level gives |  |
| <a id="railway-flow-penalty-per-damaged"></a> RAILWAY\_FLOW\_PENALTY\_PER\_DAMAGED | 5.0 | penalty to flow per damaged railway |  |
| <a id="railway-min-flow"></a> RAILWAY\_MIN\_FLOW | 5.0 | minimum railway flow can be reduced to |  |
| <a id="naval-base-flow"></a> NAVAL\_BASE\_FLOW | 5.0 | used for calculating "flow" from a naval node to another naval node when it is connected via a convoy route NAVAL\_BASE\_MAX\_SUPPLY\_FLOW\_FACTOR = 0.9, -- flow of the parent node is factored to this ratio (so at most it can transfer parent naval node flow \* this define) max output/input of a naval node is limited by this base value + additional ratio for each level |  |
| <a id="naval-flow-per-level"></a> NAVAL\_FLOW\_PER\_LEVEL | 3.0 | max output/input of a naval node is limited by previous base value + this define per its level |  |
| <a id="supply-node-min-supply-threshold"></a> SUPPLY\_NODE\_MIN\_SUPPLY\_THRESHOLD | 1.0 | if supply of a node is below this value it will be set to 0 -- Currently unused? This should happen when enough damage occurs |  |
| <a id="infra-to-supply"></a> INFRA\_TO\_SUPPLY | 0.3 | each level of infra gives this many supply |  |
| <a id="vp-to-supply-base"></a> VP\_TO\_SUPPLY\_BASE | 0.2 | Bonus to supply from a VP, no matter the level |  |
| <a id="vp-to-supply-bonus-conversion"></a> VP\_TO\_SUPPLY\_BONUS\_CONVERSION | 0.05 | Bonus to supply local supplies from Victory Points, multiplied by this aspect and rounded to closest integer |  |
| <a id="supply-from-damaged-infra"></a> SUPPLY\_FROM\_DAMAGED\_INFRA | 0.15 | damaged infrastructure counts as this in supply calcs |  |
| <a id="supply-base-mult"></a> SUPPLY\_BASE\_MULT | 0.2 | multiplier on supply base values |  |
| <a id="supply-disruption-daily-recovery"></a> SUPPLY\_DISRUPTION\_DAILY\_RECOVERY | 1.5 | every day nodes recover this much of their accumulated disruption. |  |
| <a id="railway-conversion-cooldown"></a> RAILWAY\_CONVERSION\_COOLDOWN | 10 | railways will be put on cooldown when they are captured by enemy and will not be usable during the cooldown |  |
| <a id="railway-conversion-cooldown-core"></a> RAILWAY\_CONVERSION\_COOLDOWN\_CORE | 5 |  |  |
| <a id="railway-conversion-cooldown-civilwar"></a> RAILWAY\_CONVERSION\_COOLDOWN\_CIVILWAR | 0 |  |  |
| <a id="default-starting-truck-ratio"></a> DEFAULT\_STARTING\_TRUCK\_RATIO | 1.5 | countries get this ratio of starting truck in their buffers compared to their need |  |
| <a id="default-starting-train-ratio"></a> DEFAULT\_STARTING\_TRAIN\_RATIO | 1 | countries get this ratio of starting trains in their buffers compared to their need |  |
| <a id="supply-points-per-train"></a> SUPPLY\_POINTS\_PER\_TRAIN | 1.0 | old default 1.25 -- Amount of supply that can fit in a train. (Trains distribute supply from capital to a supply node.) |  |
| <a id="num-railways-train-factor"></a> NUM\_RAILWAYS\_TRAIN\_FACTOR | 0.03 | the train usage is scaled by railway distance between the supply node and the capital multiplied by this factor |  |
| <a id="base-supply-mult-for-truck-default-buffer"></a> BASE\_SUPPLY\_MULT\_FOR\_TRUCK\_DEFAULT\_BUFFER | 1.0 | initial value for wanted buffers over potential truck usage |  |
| <a id="base-supply-mult-for-truck-min-buffer"></a> BASE\_SUPPLY\_MULT\_FOR\_TRUCK\_MIN\_BUFFER | 0.0 | min and max values for buffer ratio |  |
| <a id="base-supply-mult-for-truck-max-buffer"></a> BASE\_SUPPLY\_MULT\_FOR\_TRUCK\_MAX\_BUFFER | 100.0 |  |  |
| <a id="truck-attrition"></a> TRUCK\_ATTRITION | 0.003 | base truck attrition |  |
| <a id="truck-attrition-factor"></a> TRUCK\_ATTRITION\_FACTOR | 0.65 | a scale on total truck attrition |  |
| <a id="base-truck-hp"></a> BASE\_TRUCK\_HP | 100.0 |  |  |
| <a id="truck-hp-per-armor"></a> TRUCK\_HP\_PER\_ARMOR | 2 |  |  |
| <a id="base-train-hp"></a> BASE\_TRAIN\_HP | 100.0 |  |  |
| <a id="train-armor-targeting-weight"></a> TRAIN\_ARMOR\_TARGETING\_WEIGHT | 0.01 | For each health point gained by armor\_value, enemy bombers are this much more likely to target |  |
| <a id="train-anti-air-hit-chance"></a> TRAIN\_ANTI\_AIR\_HIT\_CHANCE | 0.07 | Balancing value to determine the chance of train anti-air hitting an attacking airwing. |  |
| <a id="train-anti-air-hit-roll-count"></a> TRAIN\_ANTI\_AIR\_HIT\_ROLL\_COUNT | 12 | The air\_attack of all attacked trains are accumulated, and then we do this many random rolls each with the hit chance set above to determine the fraction of the accumulated air\_attack that hits. |  |
| <a id="train-anti-air-attack-to-amount"></a> TRAIN\_ANTI\_AIR\_ATTACK\_TO\_AMOUNT | 0.001 | Balancing value to convert the hitting air\_attack to a percentage value of the attacking planes that are killed. |  |
| <a id="min-train-supply-factor"></a> MIN\_TRAIN\_SUPPLY\_FACTOR | 0.5 | Having 0 trains in stockpile only applies this penalty factor, scaling up to 1.0 when need is met |  |
| <a id="min-train-requirement"></a> MIN\_TRAIN\_REQUIREMENT | 2 | If total train need <= this, then don't apply any supply penalty, even if stockpile is insufficient |  |
| <a id="supply-flow-reduction-threshold"></a> SUPPLY\_FLOW\_REDUCTION\_THRESHOLD | 0.1 | if supply flow is lower than this, it is not applied |  |
| <a id="base-air-supply-mult-for-truck-buffer"></a> BASE\_AIR\_SUPPLY\_MULT\_FOR\_TRUCK\_BUFFER | 1.0 | following values are used for calculating potential truck usage generally potential is ~= current usage but as units moves along the map they are assigned to different nodes which adds slightly higher usage due to minimum truck needed being 1 |  |
| <a id="base-army-supply-mult-for-truck-buffer"></a> BASE\_ARMY\_SUPPLY\_MULT\_FOR\_TRUCK\_BUFFER | 1.0 |  |  |
| <a id="base-navy-supply-mult-for-truck-buffer"></a> BASE\_NAVY\_SUPPLY\_MULT\_FOR\_TRUCK\_BUFFER | 1.0 |  |  |

| <a id="local-node-base-supply-add"></a> LOCAL\_NODE\_BASE\_SUPPLY\_ADD | 0.5 |  |  |
| <a id="naval-node-base-supply-add"></a> NAVAL\_NODE\_BASE\_SUPPLY\_ADD | 0.3 |  |  |
| <a id="army-supply-ratio-starting-gain"></a> ARMY\_SUPPLY\_RATIO\_STARTING\_GAIN | 0.0 | ~end armies slowly gains and buffers supply above >100% up to their supply grace if they have efficent supply flow otherwuse they will lose up to 100% supply every day depending on how bad supply flow is |  |
| <a id="army-supply-ratio-speed-gain-per-hour"></a> ARMY\_SUPPLY\_RATIO\_SPEED\_GAIN\_PER\_HOUR | 0.01 |  |  |
| <a id="army-max-supply-ratio-gain-per-hour"></a> ARMY\_MAX\_SUPPLY\_RATIO\_GAIN\_PER\_HOUR | 0.15 |  |  |
| <a id="min-surrender-limit-to-move-supply-capital"></a> MIN\_SURRENDER\_LIMIT\_TO\_MOVE\_SUPPLY\_CAPITAL | 0.15 | country needs to be above thos surrender ratio to be able to move its capital |  |
| <a id="cooldown-days-after-moving-supply-capital"></a> COOLDOWN\_DAYS\_AFTER\_MOVING\_SUPPLY\_CAPITAL | 30 | cooldown for moving supply again after last move |  |
| <a id="days-to-start-giving-supply-after-moving-supply-capital"></a> DAYS\_TO\_START\_GIVING\_SUPPLY\_AFTER\_MOVING\_SUPPLY\_CAPITAL | 7 | the country will start gaining supply after this many days moving its capital |  |
| <a id="days-to-start-giving-full-supply-after-moving-supply-capital"></a> DAYS\_TO\_START\_GIVING\_FULL\_SUPPLY\_AFTER\_MOVING\_SUPPLY\_CAPITAL | 21 | the country will reach max supply after this many days moving its capital |  |
| <a id="min-diff-for-auto-updating-existing-railways"></a> MIN\_DIFF\_FOR\_AUTO\_UPDATING\_EXISTING\_RAILWAYS | 5 | while building railways, the system will prefer updating existing railway if new railway is close enough to existing one |  |
| <a id="supply-path-max-distance"></a> SUPPLY\_PATH\_MAX\_DISTANCE | 15 | reinforcements depends on distance to capital and following defines are used for calculating reinforcement time max time it can take |  |
| <a id="railway-distance-factor-for-reinforcement-speed"></a> RAILWAY\_DISTANCE\_FACTOR\_FOR\_REINFORCEMENT\_SPEED | 0.3 | time factor for total railway distance |  |
| <a id="truck-distance-factor-for-reinforcement-speed"></a> TRUCK\_DISTANCE\_FACTOR\_FOR\_REINFORCEMENT\_SPEED | 0.01 | time factor for total truck distance |  |
| <a id="naval-distance-factor-for-reinforcement-speed"></a> NAVAL\_DISTANCE\_FACTOR\_FOR\_REINFORCEMENT\_SPEED | 0.08 | time factor for total naval distance |  |
| <a id="alert-very-low-supply-level"></a> ALERT\_VERY\_LOW\_SUPPLY\_LEVEL | 0.2 | At which point we show up the low and very low supply level alert. Value is in % of supplies supported vs required. |  |
| <a id="alert-low-supply-level"></a> ALERT\_LOW\_SUPPLY\_LEVEL | 0.5 |  |  |
| <a id="ai-front-minimum-units-per-province-for-supply-calculations"></a> AI\_FRONT\_MINIMUM\_UNITS\_PER\_PROVINCE\_FOR\_SUPPLY\_CALCULATIONS | 1 | AI will try to keep this amount of divisions per province as a minimum when evaluating supply limitations for war fronts |  |
| <a id="ai-front-divisions-per-supply-point"></a> AI\_FRONT\_DIVISIONS\_PER\_SUPPLY\_POINT | 1.0 | How many divisions should the AI consider it can supply per available supply point |  |
| <a id="ai-front-max-units-enemy-count-factor"></a> AI\_FRONT\_MAX\_UNITS\_ENEMY\_COUNT\_FACTOR | 1.2 | Make sure AI front MaxNrUnits is at least EnemyCount multiplied by this factor |  |

| <a id="stored-supply-consumption-rate-factor"></a> STORED\_SUPPLY\_CONSUMPTION\_RATE\_FACTOR | 0.75 | Multiplies consumption rate of stored supply (more/less easement) |  |

## <a id="naitheatre"></a>NAITheatre
| Name | Default | Developer comment | Usage |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| <a id="ai-theatre-generation-home-theatre-depth-restriction"></a> AI\_THEATRE\_GENERATION\_HOME\_THEATRE\_DEPTH\_RESTRICTION | 2 | The home theatre is generated based off a initial depth restriction |  |
| <a id="ai-theatre-generation-border-size-restriction"></a> AI\_THEATRE\_GENERATION\_BORDER\_SIZE\_RESTRICTION | 7 | Theatres are generated based off borders, Higher value means larger theatres |  |
| <a id="ai-theatre-generation-depth-to-start-considering-borderstates"></a> AI\_THEATRE\_GENERATION\_DEPTH\_TO\_START\_CONSIDERING\_BORDERSTATES | 2 | Distance from capital in terms of states |  |
| <a id="ai-theatre-generation-minimum-state-count"></a> AI\_THEATRE\_GENERATION\_MINIMUM\_STATE\_COUNT | 3 | Small Theatres - Minimum state count for a theatre |  |
| <a id="ai-theatre-generation-max-distance-to-merge"></a> AI\_THEATRE\_GENERATION\_MAX\_DISTANCE\_TO\_MERGE | 200 | Small Theatres - Dont merge with too far away theatres, higher value means less merging will occur |  |
| <a id="ai-theatre-generation-max-distance-to-fill"></a> AI\_THEATRE\_GENERATION\_MAX\_DISTANCE\_TO\_FILL | 350 | Final generation step - Max distance to fill states, higher values means less theatres |  |
| <a id="ai-theatre-distribution-same-theatre-score-modifier"></a> AI\_THEATRE\_DISTRIBUTION\_SAME\_THEATRE\_SCORE\_MODIFIER | 0.25 | Value that affects the score of units when distributing to fronts within the same theatre, its a percentage multiplier, the higher it is the higher the chance of units staying in close proximity |  |
| <a id="ai-theatre-distribution-max-score"></a> AI\_THEATRE\_DISTRIBUTION\_MAX\_SCORE | 250000 | Max Score that a unit can have when being distributed to ai fronts, higher value means more granularity in score changes, lower values means less variation in where units can go |  |
| <a id="ai-theatre-distribution-percentage-of-minimum-units-to-keep"></a> AI\_THEATRE\_DISTRIBUTION\_PERCENTAGE\_OF\_MINIMUM\_UNITS\_TO\_KEEP | 1.0 | How much should a frontline adheer to its minimum unit demand, when removing/reassigning units |  |
| <a id="ai-theatre-distribution-max-percent-unmet-demand-per-front"></a> AI\_THEATRE\_DISTRIBUTION\_MAX\_PERCENT\_UNMET\_DEMAND\_PER\_FRONT | 0.5 | Percentage of how much fronts should request from other lower priority fronts, 0 means once a front gets hold of a unit it stays there forever until its demand is reduced, controlls shuffling of units. |  |
| <a id="ai-theatre-state-update-max-state-count-to-expand"></a> AI\_THEATRE\_STATE\_UPDATE\_MAX\_STATE\_COUNT\_TO\_EXPAND | 25 | Max theatre size |  |
| <a id="ai-theatre-breakdown-min-state-count"></a> AI\_THEATRE\_BREAKDOWN\_MIN\_STATE\_COUNT | 3 | Theatres below this size will break and merge with others |  |
| <a id="ai-theatre-breakdown-max-distance-to-merge"></a> AI\_THEATRE\_BREAKDOWN\_MAX\_DISTANCE\_TO\_MERGE | 200 | Dont merge with too far away theatres, higher value means less merging will occur |  |
| <a id="ai-theatre-percentage-of-units-to-keep-in-neighbor-defensive-orders"></a> AI\_THEATRE\_PERCENTAGE\_OF\_UNITS\_TO\_KEEP\_IN\_NEIGHBOR\_DEFENSIVE\_ORDERS | 0.05 | Percentage of units to keep in neighbor defensive orders from war fronts |  |
| <a id="ai-theatre-search-supply-node-max-depth"></a> AI\_THEATRE\_SEARCH\_SUPPLY\_NODE\_MAX\_DEPTH | 5 | Max depth of breadth-first search while looking for supply nodes when out of supply |  |
| <a id="ai-theatre-supply-crisis-limit"></a> AI\_THEATRE\_SUPPLY\_CRISIS\_LIMIT | 0.1 | If a unit is standing in an area with this supply ratio it will try to escape |  |
| <a id="ai-theatre-ai-front-min-desired-ratio"></a> AI\_THEATRE\_AI\_FRONT\_MIN\_DESIRED\_RATIO | 0.18 | Fronts are sorted based on priority, we nudge unit demand based on this sorting, the higher the value the more units the most important front gets |  |

## <a id="nindustrialorganisation"></a>NIndustrialOrganisation
| Name | Default | Developer comment | Usage |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| <a id="assign-design-team-pp-cost-per-day"></a> ASSIGN\_DESIGN\_TEAM\_PP\_COST\_PER\_DAY | 0.1 | Cost in Political Power daily generation when one MIO is assigned to a research slot. If 0, cost is entirely disabled. |  |
| <a id="assign-industrial-manufacturer-pp-cost-per-day"></a> ASSIGN\_INDUSTRIAL\_MANUFACTURER\_PP\_COST\_PER\_DAY | 0.0 | Cost in Political Power daily generation when one MIO is assigned to a production line. If 0, cost is entirely disabled. |  |
| <a id="funds-for-size-up"></a> FUNDS\_FOR\_SIZE\_UP | 700 | Funds needed for a MIO to increment its size and get points to unlock traits |  |
| <a id="funds-for-size-up-level-factor"></a> FUNDS\_FOR\_SIZE\_UP\_LEVEL\_FACTOR | 100 | How much each level mutliplies the funds for size up |  |
| <a id="funds-for-size-up-level-pow"></a> FUNDS\_FOR\_SIZE\_UP\_LEVEL\_POW | 1.8 | the power we applie to the mio size when calculating funds to level up. |  |
| <a id="unlocked-traits-per-size-up"></a> UNLOCKED\_TRAITS\_PER\_SIZE\_UP | 1 | Number of points for unlocking traits obtained when the MIO increments its size |  |
| <a id="design-team-change-xp-cost"></a> DESIGN\_TEAM\_CHANGE\_XP\_COST | 0 | Flat cost added to the XP cost of a new equipment design. If 0, cost is entirely disabled. |  |
| <a id="funds-for-research-completion-per-research-cost"></a> FUNDS\_FOR\_RESEARCH\_COMPLETION\_PER\_RESEARCH\_COST | 500 | Funds added to MIO when the Design Team has completed a research, multiplied by research\_cost in technology template |  |
| <a id="funds-for-creating-equipment-variant"></a> FUNDS\_FOR\_CREATING\_EQUIPMENT\_VARIANT | 0 | Funds added to MIO when a new variant is created with the Design Team assigned to it |  |
| <a id="funds-from-manufacturer-per-ic-per-day"></a> FUNDS\_FROM\_MANUFACTURER\_PER\_IC\_PER\_DAY | 0.1 | Funds added to MIO when a manufacturer is attached to a production line. Added every day proportional to IC produced. |  |
| <a id="max-funds-from-manufacturer-per-day"></a> MAX\_FUNDS\_FROM\_MANUFACTURER\_PER\_DAY | 100 | Max funds generated per manufacturer per day. Set to 0 for no Maximum. |  |
| <a id="design-team-research-bonus"></a> DESIGN\_TEAM\_RESEARCH\_BONUS | 0.05 | Research bonus for applying a Design Team that matches the technology |  |
| <a id="enable-task-capacity"></a> ENABLE\_TASK\_CAPACITY | false | Enable limited task capacity for MIOs |  |
| <a id="default-initial-task-capacity"></a> DEFAULT\_INITIAL\_TASK\_CAPACITY | 0 | Default start task capacity for each MIO (may be overriden in DB) |  |
| <a id="default-initial-policy-attach-cost"></a> DEFAULT\_INITIAL\_POLICY\_ATTACH\_COST | 25 | Default start attach cost in PP for policies |  |
| <a id="default-initial-attach-policy-cooldown"></a> DEFAULT\_INITIAL\_ATTACH\_POLICY\_COOLDOWN | 180 | Default start cooldown in days after attaching a policy |  |
| <a id="legacy-cost-factor-scale"></a> LEGACY\_COST\_FACTOR\_SCALE | 1.0 | Multiplier to use when legacy Designer cost factors is applied to MIOs (<IdeaGroup>\_cost\_factor) |  |

| DEFAULT\_PROJECT\_COMPLETION\_SCIENTIST\_EXPERIENCE\_GAIN | 192.0 | Default experience gain for assigned scientist when a project is completed |  |

| SCIENTIST\_BASIC\_RESEARCH\_DAILY\_XP\_GAIN | 0.28 | Daily experience gain for doing basic research |  |
| RECRUIT\_SCIENTIST\_COST | {25, 50, 75, 100} | pp cost if no available scientist pp cost if 1 available scientist pp cost if 2 available scientist pp cost if more than 2 available scientist | Amount of pp to hire a scientist based on available scientist |
| SCIENTIST\_SKILL\_LEVEL\_THRESHOLDS | {100, 100, 300, 700, 1500} | to go from level 0 to level 1 to go from level 1 to level 2 to go from level 2 to level 3 ... Max level = Array size | Threshold for scientist to level up |
| SCIENTIST\_SKILL\_LEVEL\_SPEED\_MODIFIER | {-1.0, -0.05, 0.05, 0.1, 0.15, 0.25\| | -1.0 means -100%         also name loc key is SCIENTIST\_SKILL\_LEVEL\_NAME\_0 -0.05 means -5%            also name loc key is SCIENTIST\_SKILL\_LEVEL\_NAME\_1 0 means no change        also name loc key is SCIENTIST\_SKILL\_LEVEL\_NAME\_2 0.15 means +15%         ... -- Size MUST be SCIENTIST\_SKILL\_LEVEL\_THRESHOLDS's size + 1 | Bonus to apply to daily phase progress according to the skill level of the scientist |
| PROJECT\_LOSS\_FACTOR\_ON\_CAPTURE | 0.2 | Factor of lost progress on project when facility is captured |  |
| PROJECT\_CAPTURE\_GAIN\_RATIO | 0.2 | Ratio of difference from captured facilities ongoing project to receive to the captors' progress |  |
| PROJECT\_CAPTURE\_BREAKTHROUGH\_PROGRESS | 0.1 | Ratio of breakthrough progress on capture to the captor for the facilities specialization |  |
| PROJECT\_CAPTURE\_DIMINISHING\_RETURN | 0.6 | Reduced amount of gain when capturing a facility with a project you already gained. Will apply the factor each time a capture occurs. 0.6 means a reduction of 60% on next project capture. |  |
| BASIC\_RESEARCH\_TECHNOLOGY\_BONUS\_FACTOR | 0.02 | Bonus research factor applied to technologies per scientist skill level when performing basic research in a matching facility. |  |
| BASIC\_RESEARCH\_TECHNOLOGY\_BONUS\_DIMINISHING\_RETURN\_FACTOR | 0.5 | Diminishing return on BASIC\_RESEARCH\_TECHNOLOGY\_BONUS\_FACTOR for each extra scientist performing basic research for multiple facilities. |  |
| BREAKTHROUGH\_DAILY\_TECHNOLOGY\_GAIN | 12 | Amount in 1/100th percentage. E.g. 25 = 0.25% |  |
| BREAKTHROUGH\_DAILY\_SCIENTIST\_SKILL\_GAIN | 5 | Amount in 1/100th percentage gained per skill when doing basic research. E.g. 5 = 0.05% per skill level. |  |
| BREAKTHROUGH\_DAILY\_ROCKET\_SITE\_GAIN | 1 | Amount in 1/100th percentage gained per rocket site level. E.g. 1 = 0.01% per rocket site level. |  |
| BREAKTHROUGH\_DAILY\_NUCLEAR\_REACTOR\_GAIN | 1 | Amount in 1/100th percentage gained per nuclear reactor. E.g. 2 = 0.02% per nuclear reactor. |  |
| BREAKTHROUGH\_GAIN\_ANIMATION\_SPEED\_MAX | 1.0 | The animation for gaining breakthrough progress is a ratio of this value and current daily gain. |  |

## <a id="nairgfx"></a>NAirGfx
| Name | Default | Developer comment | Usage |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| <a id="airplanes-animation-global-speed-per-gamespeed"></a> AIRPLANES\_ANIMATION\_GLOBAL\_SPEED\_PER\_GAMESPEED | { 0.22, 0.28, 0.32, 0.38, 0.44, 0.5 } | Speed factor for each game speed (begin with paused). Larger value = faster animation. |  |
| <a id="rocket-speed"></a> ROCKET\_SPEED | 15.0 | Speed of rockets launched from rocket sites |  |
| <a id="airplanes-curve-point-density"></a> AIRPLANES\_CURVE\_POINT\_DENSITY | 2.0 | LOWER value = more midpoints in the flight path. |  |
| <a id="airplanes-curve-max-extrapolation"></a> AIRPLANES\_CURVE\_MAX\_EXTRAPOLATION | 20.0 | It's the limit value that avoid making gigantic curves that may happen when flight path is very long. |  |
| <a id="airplanes-curve-min-elevation"></a> AIRPLANES\_CURVE\_MIN\_ELEVATION | 4.0 | Minimum height above the ground that the curve will generate it's points. Excludes first and last point (takeoff/landing). |  |
| <a id="airplanes-scale-takeoff-dist"></a> AIRPLANES\_SCALE\_TAKEOFF\_DIST | 0.1 | Until first x% of the flight path, the airplane will scale up. |  |
| <a id="airplanes-scale-min"></a> AIRPLANES\_SCALE\_MIN | 0.1 | Minimum airplane scale down when takeoff/landing. |  |
| <a id="airplanes-scale-landing-dist"></a> AIRPLANES\_SCALE\_LANDING\_DIST | 0.9 | After last x% of the flight path, the airplane will scale down. |  |
| <a id="airplanes-smooth-interpolation-move"></a> AIRPLANES\_SMOOTH\_INTERPOLATION\_MOVE | 0.13 | How smooth is the movement interpolation. |  |
| <a id="airplanes-smooth-interpolation-turn"></a> AIRPLANES\_SMOOTH\_INTERPOLATION\_TURN | 0.12 | How smooth is the turning interpolation. |  |
| <a id="airplanes-bank-strength"></a> AIRPLANES\_BANK\_STRENGTH | 210.0 | Multiplier of how much the curve affects the wings banking. (angle limited by the following value) |  |
| <a id="airplanes-bank-angle-limit"></a> AIRPLANES\_BANK\_ANGLE\_LIMIT | 55.0 | Bank angle limit. |  |
| <a id="airplanes-ground-collision-offset-y"></a> AIRPLANES\_GROUND\_COLLISION\_OFFSET\_Y | 0.0 | Set's the height (Y) offset before 3d airplanes disappear after going to the ground. |  |
| <a id="airplanes-ground-explosion-time-delay"></a> AIRPLANES\_GROUND\_EXPLOSION\_TIME\_DELAY | 0.6 | Time in seconds to play explosion animation when plane hit ground before the plane entity is deleted |  |
| <a id="airplanes-1-fighter-patrol-anim"></a> AIRPLANES\_1\_FIGHTER\_PATROL\_ANIM | 1 | Number of fighters needed for a single instance of this animation |  |
| <a id="airplanes-3-fighter-patrol-anim"></a> AIRPLANES\_3\_FIGHTER\_PATROL\_ANIM | 3 | Number of fighters needed for a single instance of this animation |  |

## <a id="ncareerprofile"></a>NCareerProfile
| Name | Default | Developer comment | Usage |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| <a id="mod-statistics-group"></a> MOD\_STATISTICS\_GROUP | "" | Mod defines Can be set by mods to collect statistics in a separate data set for the mod. Will also be used as the display name if MOD\_STATISTICS\_GROUP\_NAME is not set. |  |
| <a id="mod-statistics-group-name"></a> MOD\_STATISTICS\_GROUP\_NAME | "" | Can be set by mods as a display name for the mod's statistics data set. It can be a localized. |  |
| <a id="naval-invasion-medal-max-duration"></a> NAVAL\_INVASION\_MEDAL\_MAX\_DURATION | 96 | Statistics parameters Maximum duration in hours to finish naval invasion and get a Naval Invasion Medal |  |
| <a id="paradrop-award-division-min-battalion-count"></a> PARADROP\_AWARD\_DIVISION\_MIN\_BATTALION\_COUNT | 5 | Minimum count of battalions in the division required to count that division for paradrop awards ("Paradrop Medal" and "They came from Above") |  |
| <a id="naval-invasion-medal-division-min-battalion-count"></a> NAVAL\_INVASION\_MEDAL\_DIVISION\_MIN\_BATTALION\_COUNT | 5 | Minimum count of battalions in the division required to count that division for Naval Invasion Medal |  |
| <a id="turning-tide-medal-division-min-battalion-count"></a> TURNING\_TIDE\_MEDAL\_DIVISION\_MIN\_BATTALION\_COUNT | 5 | Minimum count of battalions in the division required to count that division for Turning the Tide Medal |  |
| <a id="lord-of-the-seas-medal-min-supremacy"></a> LORD\_OF\_THE\_SEAS\_MEDAL\_MIN\_SUPREMACY | 0.75 | Minimum supremacy to count current naval region for Lord of the Seas Medal |  |
| <a id="steel-at-high-speed-ribbon-tank-speed"></a> STEEL\_AT\_HIGH\_SPEED\_RIBBON\_TANK\_SPEED | 12 | Minimum speed to count deployed tanks for Steel at High Speed Ribbon |  |
| <a id="orchestra-of-boom-ribbon-special-battalion-count"></a> ORCHESTRA\_OF\_BOOM\_RIBBON\_SPECIAL\_BATTALION\_COUNT | 4 | Amount of special battalion types(anti-air, anti-tank, artillery and rocket artillery) required for the division for Orchestra of Boom Ribbon |  |
| <a id="nevermine-me-medal-min-supremacy-effect"></a> NEVERMINE\_ME\_MEDAL\_MIN\_SUPREMACY\_EFFECT | 0.5 | Minimum effect mines should have on the supremacy to count current naval region for Nevermine Me Medal |  |
| <a id="blitz-this-tactic-name"></a> BLITZ\_THIS\_TACTIC\_NAME | "tactic\_elastic\_defense" | The tactic required to be applied to a leader or a country for Blitz This Ribbon |  |
| <a id="engineering-behemoth-medal-armor-rating-bronze"></a> ENGINEERING\_BEHEMOTH\_MEDAL\_ARMOR\_RATING\_BRONZE | 100 | The armor rating required for the tanks to get the Engineering The Behemoth Bronze Medal |  |
| <a id="engineering-behemoth-medal-armor-rating-silver"></a> ENGINEERING\_BEHEMOTH\_MEDAL\_ARMOR\_RATING\_SILVER | 160 | The armor rating required for the tanks to get the Engineering The Behemoth Silver Medal |  |
| <a id="engineering-behemoth-medal-armor-rating-gold"></a> ENGINEERING\_BEHEMOTH\_MEDAL\_ARMOR\_RATING\_GOLD | 200 | The armor rating required for the tanks to get the Engineering The Behemoth Gold Medal |  |
| <a id="castles-in-the-air-medal-air-defense-bronze"></a> CASTLES\_IN\_THE\_AIR\_MEDAL\_AIR\_DEFENSE\_BRONZE | 20 | The air defense required for the airplanes to get the Castles in the Air Bronze Medal |  |
| <a id="castles-in-the-air-medal-air-defense-silver"></a> CASTLES\_IN\_THE\_AIR\_MEDAL\_AIR\_DEFENSE\_SILVER | 50 | The air defense required for the airplanes to get the Castles in the Air Silver Medal |  |
| <a id="castles-in-the-air-medal-air-defense-gold"></a> CASTLES\_IN\_THE\_AIR\_MEDAL\_AIR\_DEFENSE\_GOLD | 100 | The air defense required for the airplanes to get the Castles in the Air Gold Medal |  |

| <a id="career-points-animation-duration"></a> CAREER\_POINTS\_ANIMATION\_DURATION | 950 | Count the career points up for this many milliseconds |  |
